… SF is more than that.

/*Science Fiction*/ (often called sci-fi or SF) is a popular genre of
fiction in which the narrative world differs from our own present or
historical reality in at least one significant way. This difference may
be technological, physical, historical, sociological, philosophical,
metaphysical, etc, but not magical (see Fantasy).

—Excerpted from Science Fiction
<http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Science_Fiction> on /Wikipedia/, the Free
Encyclopedia.

Science Fiction books from before the 20th century are listed on the
page Precursors of Science Fiction
<https://www.gutenberg.org/wiki/Precursors_of_Science_Fiction_(Bookshelf)>.
The cutoff is more by author than by date. Jules Verne (1828-1905) is
usually considered the first modern SF author.

Additional titles available through catalog search
<https://www.gutenberg.org/ebooks/search/%3Fquery%3Ds.science%2Bfiction%2B!%2BbsxScience%2B!%2BbsxFiction>.


Feel free to add reviews of books to the page (wiki login
<https://www.gutenberg.org/wiki/Special:UserLogin>).

The Project Gutenberg Science Fiction CD is is available via BitTorrent
from The Project Gutenberg BitTorrent Tracker
<http://snowy.arsc.alaska.edu:6969/>. See The CD and DVD Project:
Downloading Via BitTorrent
<https://www.gutenberg.org/wiki/Gutenberg:The_CD_and_DVD_Project#Downloading_Via_BitTorrent>.
